complex in Palm Springs. 

The unit is a 2 bedroom, 1.75 bath, single story, private end unit that has been recently renovated.  The unit features a large master bedroom with a queen size bed, including a new Simmons Beautyrest mattress and higher-end, all cotton linens.  The second bedroom has two twin beds and sleeps two comfortably.  A queen size air mattress is available for occasional guests. 

The living area features vaulted ceilings and a recently renovated kitchen that is well stocked with cooking utensils.  There is also a dining area, a comfortable living room, and in-suite laundry with a new, front loading washer and dryer.  For outdoor space, the unit features two patios, including a small patio out front, and a large, lush, fully enclosed private patio in the back with patio furniture and a BBQ.  Cable TV, wireless high speed internet, and a land line with unlimited calling to the U.S., Canada, and Puerto Rico are included in the rent.  

The complex features two tennis courts and 6 swimming pools, including one just steps away from the unit.  There are also many citrus fruit trees located around the complex, including orange, grapefruit and lemon trees located right outside the unit.  This complex is well run, has friendly neighbours, and is popular with snowbirds from across Canada and the northern U.S.

Additionally, the complex is located on Tahquitz Creek Golf Course, a public golf course with 32 holes that is managed by Arnold Palmer's management company.  The complex is also conveniently located nearby several shopping options, including Trader Joe's, Vons, Target, Wal-Mart, Home Depot, Lowes, Ross, Marshalls and more.

This unit has been well looked after and I'm looking for renters who will treat this unit like their own property, particularly as I'm located remotely in Northern California. The large yard with brand new pool and spa have mountain views from every angle. Crisp white walls, Jonathan Adler furnishings, custom draperies and pillows, and glossy 24 x 24 floor tiles all work together seamlessly to create the most beautiful backdrop that will make your vacation memorable for years to come!</div><div data-reactid="2040">LIVE MORE! is located in the neighborhood with the highest concentration of Alexander and other architecturally significant mid-century modern homes built between 1955 and 1961. This neighborhood has been remarkably preserved and restored home-by-home over the past 10+ years and now is one of the sought after communities in the city. The home has 3 bedrooms, 2 baths, and a double seating area living space with an open floor plan kitchen. This house is as easy for a couple to enjoy as a group of 6. Every room in the house has mountain views and access to the yard via large sliding doors. The walled and gated yard provides endless hours of pool side fun, multiple seating areas, and complete privacy.

The pool yard has some of the most unobstructed wrap-around mountain views available in Palm Springs. The 14’ x 28’ pool is 6’ deep and has all day long sun exposure since it’s pushed out away from the house and shade. The 6 person 7’ x 7’ spa sits above the pool with spillover waterfalls to the pool and great views of the house and San Jacinto mountains.

Living room 1, directly off the kitchen, has a sectional corner sofa and a 50” SHARP flatscreen with built in Netflix, Sling, HBO NOW, and amazon prime video apps (you need your own accounts) – as well as Time Warner Cable. There is a retro style Victrola record player with a stack of 33’s – but if you would rather play your own music you can bring your own cd’s or hook up any smart phone or tablet via bluetooth or with the auxiliary input. There are also a stack of different playing cards, books, and board games.

Living room 2, with access to the pool, has a tuxedo style tufted bottom grey sofa, two club chairs, custom draperies and pillows, and floor lamps – perfect for mingling, enjoying a martini, or staring out at the sparkling pool and spa.

The dining room has a stunning white lacquer Jonathan Adler dining table that seats 6-8 people comfortably,  a white lacquer buffet , a fully stocked bar serving cart (just bring your own alcohol) and groovy shag style artwork and light fixtures along with custom draperies. 

The kitchen has brand new stainless Frigidaire Gallery appliances, solid surface white counter tops, and white lacquer cabinetry. Everything you could need to prepare and serve a great meal is here and waiting for you. There is also a breakfast bar on the outside of the kitchen extended island with 2 barstools – perfect for keeping the cook company, or working on your laptop should you need to.

The oversized master bedroom has a queen bed, a 50” SHARP flatscreen with built in Netflix, sling, HBO NOW, and amazon prime video apps – as well as Time Warner Cable. This bedroom has large en suite bathroom with dual sinks and a large walk in shower stall with 10” rain shower head and clerestory window that allows for palm tree views and tons of natural light. This bedroom also has a walk in closet flooded with natural light through the round porthole window with Southern exposure.

Guest bedroom 1 has a full bed and wall to wall mirrored closet doors. This room has a 40” Samsung flatscreen with Time Warner Cable and sliding door access to the pool yard.

Guest bedroom 2 has two standard twin beds and wall to wall mirrored closet doors. This room has a  “32” Insignia flatscreen tv with Time Warner Cable and sliding door access to the pool yard.

The guest bathroom at the end of the hall – shared by the two guest bedrooms – has a wide double sink vanity and a large step in shower with a clear frameless glass enclosure.

data-reactid="2173"><!-- react-text: 2174 --><!-- /react-text --><div data-reactid="2175">Villa San Jacinto is a private single level luxury condominium centrally located within a gated compound in Palm Springs, California. Come relax and enjoy yourself in this spacious and well appointed condominium home. A Two bedroom, Two bath end villa with sweeping 360 degree mountain views. Close to Tennis Courts, Hot Tub and Swimming Pools.
Villa San Jacinto is the perfect combination for a comfortable, carefree and relaxing vacation in the desert. This villa is perfect in every detail. There are eight swimming pools. Four tennis courts. Twenty four hour security. Large hot tub spa. Putting green and recreation center. The villa has privacy like that of a single family residence. Surrounded by Golf courses, Park lands and Indian reservations. Expansive mountain views and over three hundred days of sun a year make this a real getaway for fun in the sun. Conveniently located in Palm Springs just five minutes from the international airport and major shopping. Downtown Palm Springs is less than ten minutes away.
Villa San Jacinto is adjacent to Tahquitz Creek Golf Resort and near Knott's Soak City water park
The villa is available to rent by the week or month.
Amenities include:
Cable TV, High Speed Internet WiFi. Blu-ray entertainment system. Flat screen TV's in Living room and both bedrooms.
Tiled Patio with lounge seating, dining table and gas bar-b-q
Large Living room and Dining room with ten foot high vaulted ceilings.
Well appointed gourmet Kitchen with new stainless appliances and Corian counter tops
Large bedrooms with comfortable pillow top beds.
Original Contemporary Art throughout.
Upgraded custom furnishings.
Washer, Dryer, iron and ironing board.
Sports equipment, Bikes, Tennis rackets, Golf putters etc.
Private covered parking and guest parking located right at the entry
Upgraded bed and bath linens.  
Villa San Jacinto is an Ideal destination for year round travelers of all ages.
 Come stay at our villa. You'll come back again and again!
